Wa ɣef umedyaz, wa ɣef umengal, wa ɣef unallas, wa ɣef umsezgun.
Cwiṭ cwiṭ, ad nesbedd amezruy n tsekla-nneɣ.
Ad nesbedd taqbaylit-nneɣ.
Ayen-nniḍen, yal wa d ṛṛay-is.
Ṣṣenf n udlis-agi, mačči d ayen isehlen ad t-yexdem yiwen.
D ayen iḥwaǧen akud d trusi n leɛqel d tezmert.
Ilaq isefra ad ten-id-yejmeɛ umdan, yiwen yiwen.
Ad ten-id-isbin belli n umedyaz Saɛid Ucemmut.
Ad ten-yaru, ad ten-isismel, ad ten-yesleḍ.
Ɣur-i taɣaḍt, tecfa-d i tṛad mgal Fransa.
Aɣyul-iw ijaḥ.
Ticki iẓẓan-ik d iberkanen, xas ddu ad t-waliḍ ṭbib.
Ticki llan idammen deg yibeccan-ik, azzel ar twaliḍ amejjay.
Ečč neɣ qqim, ssuma yiwet.
Acḥal yeswa kilu n uksum?
Aṭamḍan d tmenya n yibiten.
Akiluṭamḍan, d alef u rebɛa u miyya n yiṭamḍanen.
Amigaṭamḍan, d alef u rebɛa u miyya n ikiluṭamḍanen.
Yewɛer ad tegzuḍ tayunin n uktili n telɣut di tsenselkimt.
D acu-tt tsenselkimt?
Tasenselkimt d tussna tumdint tatrart.
Tasnamant d tussna icudden ar waman.
Ttif xir win ur neẓri, wala win yeẓran.
A bu snat, bru i yiwet.
Qujjreɣ seg ugris.
Zzit-a tesbek.
Qquren waman di tala.
Llexseɣ seg ugeffur.
Yekkat ugeffur deg unebdu.
Tekkat lehwa deg ccetwa neɣ tagrest.
Leɛyub n usekkil n taɛrabt ggten.
Tussda deg wawal, nettaru-tt akken i nuɣ tanumi nsell-as.
Llan wawalen ideg tella tussda deg kra n tmeslayin, maca deg tira nesmenyif talɣa war tussda.
Tussda n tergalt tamezwarut n yimyagen, tekka-d seg uɣelluy n yiwet n tergalt n zik.
Imru i ṭṭfeɣ akka tura mačči d ayla-k.
Astilu i ṭṭfeɣ akka tura mačči d ayla-k.
Imru i teṭṭfeḍ akka tura d ayla-w.
Imru i yi-d-tefka Sarah mačči d anili.
Imru i muddeɣ i Sarah d azeggaɣ.
Iqbayliyen ɣur-sen taɣerma am yiɣerfan-nniḍen.
Amzun yečča aḥeckul.
Zlu-as asfel.
Squddeṛ-as aldun, ternuḍ tḥukkeḍ-as aẓarif.
Zuzer-as taẓult ɣef lecfaṛ-is.
Ddez-as lǧuz, sakin tmuddeḍ-as ar uqemmuc.
Sefɛej-as snat tɛeqqayin n ṭumaṭic, ternuḍ-as tageggert n ticcert.
Gzem tgeggar n uẓalim, rnu-as kra n wafriwen n felyu.
Ḥku-yi-d tamahut a jeddi.
Ḥwi izgaren-ik sya.
Ɣur-k ad d-zeggreḍ talast-a.
Takfilt-a d tbut n talast acḥal d iseggasen aya.
Lliɣ ttawiɣ yid-i n makken kesseɣ deg Iɣzeṛ Tɛerqubt.
Ksiɣ acḥal d iseggasen uqbel ad kecmeɣ ar tesdawit.
Bɣiɣ ad uɣaleɣ ar teksawt.
Zik lliɣ ttandiɣ tifextin i yimerga.
Yiwet n tikkelt, ṭṭfeɣ-d ilef amecṭuḥ deg tceṛket.
Ttandiɣ daɣen taqerrut i yiẓerẓar.
Taqerrut undiɣ-tt ɣef tqacuct n teslent.
Seqdaceɣ igeḍman n uḥeccad akked lazuq ticki undiɣ taqerrut.
Ẓeṭṭeɣ tiqecwalin s tleẓẓaẓt.
Tikwal gezzmeɣ-d igeḍman n wufni.
Ufni yettmuddu-d ibawen n wuccen.
Nella nessefɛaj ibawen n wufni deg uɣerbaz akken ad tekker rriḥa, sakin ad d-neffeɣ.
S ilibuḍen i ttruḥuɣ ar uɣerbaz deg iseggasen n tmanyin.
Yiwet n tikkelt, lsiɣ sin ilibuḍen mgaraden, dɣa arrac ttaḍsan fell-i.
Ma d tikkelt, lsiɣ yiwen uqaciṛ d awraɣ, wayeḍ d azeggaɣ.
Acḥal n tikkal i wwteɣ aserwal s tfawtin, armi uɣaleɣ d taḍsa gar warrac.
Aselmad-iw n tefransist yenna-k: Kečč ilaq ad d-teffɣeḍ d ameksa.
Mi lliɣ d agrud, ttebciceɣ deg usu.
Asmi lliɣ d acawrar, ttakreɣ-d si tmizar.
Ulac tamazirt ur d-nzuṛ.
Nekka-d iqwiṛen yiwen yiwen, seg Uzemmur Umeryem arma d Buḍahaṛ.
Nerǧem ar teɛciwt n Kuku imi din i ttsikkiṛen yirgazen di tallit-nni.
Iḍfer-iyi-d yiwen urgaz, yettmala, ur yezmir ara ad ibedd seg tissit.
Nniɣ-as i Muḥ Azuran: Kečč ɛeddi s ufella, nekk ad ɛeddiɣ s wadda.
Ɛerqent-as i Saɛid Amsaḥ anwa abrid ara yaɣ.
Ma yuder yugad ad yecceḍ, ma yuli ur yezmir ara ad yazzel.
Yuḍen uqjun-iw ass-a.
Aqjun-iw yeggan akked umcic-iw.
Muddeɣ-as ayaziḍ i uqjun-iw.
Amcic-iw itezzi ɣef tecriḥt i muddeɣ i teqjunt-iw.
Iṣukk-iyi-d uɣyul-iw.
Serseɣ tineqqalin ɣef uɣyul, saki ɛebbaɣ-as snat tbettiyin n waman.
Serseɣ taberda ɣef uɣyul sakin ɛebbaɣ-as tazdemt n tleẓẓawt.
Ččureɣ-d tkata n tcekkaṛin n legric si tessirt.
Ɛemmreɣ-d azal n lqella n umuṛej si tessirt.
Zzit n Uqbu d ddwa ḥellu.
Acuɣer ḥemmlen iqbayliyen ad ddun ar Uqbu akked Sidi Ɛic?
Ugin-iyi imawlan-iw ad aɣeɣ yelli-s n Ḥemmu n At Ufella.
Tin yebɣal wul, ugin-tt imawlan.
Texla n tmurt n leqbayel.
Ilmeẓyen n tmurt n leqbayel ad regglen ara tmura tibeṛṛaniyin.
Di tefsut taberkant, iǧadaṛmiyen nɣan ddeqs n yilmeẓyen, wiyaḍ ɛeggben ilebda.
Ur ɣriɣ ara deg uɣerbaz.
Ur ssineɣ ara ad aruɣ.
Iṭurrec uberhuc-iw makken iwala aksum deg ufus-iw.
Ḥucceɣ-d tazdemt n usaɣur.
Ciddeɣ ass-a asaɣur-iw.
Megreɣ-d kra n temẓin.
Zik nteg izraren s warwari.
Rennunt tlawin afrur i talaxt akken ad tiǧhid.
Tegent tlawin lmeɣri i talaxt ticki teqqed.
Ass-a qqdeɣ-tt imi swiɣ rebɛa n yiqbucen n cṛab.
Ccix n taddart ibren-as agiṛṛu n teḥcict.
Yerḍa-tt-id.
Urḍan-is tteffuḥun.
Yebra-d i turiḍt.
Qqaṛen turiḍt neɣ uriḍ.
I uḍris-nni? Turiḍ-t?
Ih, uriɣ-t.
Nekk taddart-iw d Tawrirt At Mansuṛ.
Ad waliɣ ma zemreɣ ad d-aseɣ.
Ad aliɣ ar ssqef ad d-erreɣ tiqqit.
Ad sendiɣ i waman di tala.
Ad ferneɣ abrid ara yaɣeɣ.
Uliɣ ad d-cerweɣ tazemmurt.
Kkseɣ-d rriḥan akked sisnu.
Briɣ-as i win i k-id-yefkan.
Tesfuǧǧuɣeḍ aṭas.
Tesfuǧǧurem am uzal am yiḍ.
A lḥif-nwen ma d irgazen kenwi!
Yeqqaṛ aṭas idlisen s tefransist.
Tasekla tafransist iḍumm-itt-id meṛṛa.
Iḥemmel tudert i ttidiren yimdanen deg umaḍal utrim.
Maca yessen kan tafransist.
Ihi yega-d kra n leḥbab di Facebook d iṛumyen yettqessiṛ yid-sen.
Yiwen n wass yenna-yas-d Jack: Azul a Munir.
Munir ur yegzi kra.
Amek akka? Daɣen ttnuzun wurḍan di Fransa?
Maca ur yumin ara.
Munir yeḥrec.
Ihi uqbel ad yerr tiririt i Jack, yedda ar Google akken ad inadi d acu-t unamek-nniḍen n wawal-a.
Yufa tabadut-s di Wikamawal.
Inuda tasuqilt, dɣa yegza.
Ihi, werdin kan, Munir, mmi-s n Dda Remḍan, yerra-yas i Jack, yenna-yas: Ɣur-i taɣaṭ deg uxxam.
Jack yegdeh, sakin yenna: Igerrez a Munir.
Akken ifuk usqerdec akked Jack, Munir yenna i tmeṭṭut-is Seɛdiya: Jack yefka-yi-d tikti igerrzen aṭas.
Tenna-yas Seɛdiya: Ɛni yettmeslay uqjun n Si Caɛvan?
Yerra-yas-d Munir: Ala! Mačči d aqjun n Si Caɛvan.
Jack d amdakel-iw si Fransa.
Seɛdiya: Ɛni yella wass ideg truḥeḍ ar Fransa?
Munir: Ala, d amdakel-iw di Facebook.
Seɛdiya: Aḥlil! D amdakel di Facebook?
Ur tettenkareḍ ara ad tmuddeḍ asaɣur i taɣaṭ-nni?
Ussan-a ur d-tettmuddu ara maḍi ayefki.
Munir: Seg uzekka d afella, ur tezziɣ ara ad d-awiɣ lqut i yiqersiwen-im.
Ma tebɣiḍ zzenz-iten. Nekk ad d-aɣeɣ akanic.
Seɛdiya: Akanic? D acu-t wa?
Seɛdiya ur teɣri ara tafransist, ihi tessusem kan meskint, tɣil d kra n tɣawsiwin i uxxam.
Ɛeddan kra n wussan, Munir yuɣ-d akanic yerna-d abirmuda awezlan anect n tkiluḍt.
Ihi yexdem am akken iwala Jack di tewlafin i as-d-yuzen.
Yelsa abirmuda, yezzuɣer-d akanic s snesla, maca imi yella cwiṭ n usemmiḍ tameddit-nni, yerna yesburr-d abernus.
Ad yeteddu di taddart, armi yewweḍ ar tejmaɛit.
Irgazen yellan din wehmen.
Yenṭeq-d Yidir Umḥend: Azul a Munir, ɛni teṭṭukkiḍ. D acu-t wa?
Munir: Wagi d akanic-iw. Iḍelli i t-id-uɣeɣ.
Irgazen ṛwan taḍsa. Ɛni ttnuzun wurḍan?
Munir: Urḍan? Ala, s teglizit d aɣersiw.
Yidir: Acuɣer i telsiḍ abirmuda terniḍ tesburreḍ-d abernus?
Munir: Kenwi teggumam ad tennernim. Ahbuh!
Ihi taddart tesla, teṛwa taḍsa.
Yeffeɣ lexbaṛ ɣef Munir i d-yuɣen urḍan s yidrimen.
Seɛdiya yewweḍ-itt lexbaṛ.
Tewwi-as-t-id tmeṭṭut n Caɛvan.
Dɣa seg wass-n i as-d-eǧǧa sin n yinzan.
Am win yettṛebbin akanic, ulac taduṭ, ulac rric.
Am mmi-s n Dda Remḍan, yefkan idrimen deg wurḍan.
Ma d tikkelt-nniḍen, aselmad-is n teqbaylit, yewwi-d aḍris ɣef ukanic n Mass Ǧeḥḥa.
Meẓyan ur yegzi kra.
Amek amdan ad iteddu ad ileqqeḍ iẓẓan n ukanic-is di beṛṛa?
Amek akka amdan ad yeggan akked ukanic deg usu?
Amek akka amdan deg umḍiq ad yerr agrud ɣer dduḥ, d akanic ara yeṭṭfen amḍiq n ugrud?
Dɣa Meẓyan yuɣal yekreh tamsirt n tutlayt taqbaylit.
Iɣunza-tt. Seg wassen ur yezzi ad iɣer adlis s teqbaylit.
Meẓyan d aqcic n xemsa n yiseggasen.
Yekcem ar uɣerbaz n tyemmat akken ad yebdu taɣuri send ad yekcem ar uɣerbaz amenzu.
Deg uɣerbaz yeqqaṛ snat n tutlayin: Tafransist akked taqbaylit.
Yiwen n wass deg wussan n Ṛebbi, aselmad-is n tefransist yewwi-as-d aḍris ɣef taɣaṭ n Mass Segin.
Meẓyan yewhem.
Segmi yeqqaṛ aḍris, yettaf iman-is.
Iḥulfa am akken taqsiḍt-a teḍra-d deg taddart-is.
Dɣa yuɣal iḥemmel tafransist.
Ɣriɣ tamahut n uɛeqqa yessawalen.
Zik baba, iḥekku-yaɣ-d timicuha ɣef yiri n lkanun.
Yemma tella tẓeṭṭ iɛlawen, tiḥuyak akked ibernyas.
Yemma tella tmessel tiqbucin, tisebbalin, tibaqiyin, akked ifeṛṛaḥen.
Ticki tsiɣ yemma times, tesrusuy inyen ɣef lkanun, sakin ad tessert tuggict.
Tikwal nsewway baṭaṭa di lkanun.
Baba daɣen yettawi-d abelluḍ, yeggar-it ar yirij akken ad yezzu.
Nekni neggar ar tmes iɛuras akken ad ten-nečč.
Nettekkes-d tigerselin seg tiẓgi sakin neggar-iten ar yirij.

Di Tala Gilef i sekkṛeɣ tikelt tamezwarut.
Yeḥzen uɣyul, azger yuɣ rrif.
Iserwula udren, ad ẓuɣuren ikanicen.
Yebna-tt uɣyul, yečča-tt ukanic.

D acu i d taynisemt?

Acu kan ɣezzif azuḥ!

Ayen i d-nnan imsulɣa akked deg isegzawalen.
Ayen i d-nnan akk imyura.
Seg tilin n umdan ɣer wass-a, ad naf d akken amdan yettidir d igrawen neɣ d tagruma deg yiwen n wadeg.

Ad nesseqḍeɛ ajenwi akken ad nezlu axeṛfi.

D acu i tettnadi-ḍ ay aderɣal? D tafat.
Ẓriɣ, ad yuɣal ad yelmed belli irgazen mačči d iḥeqqiyen akkit, belli mačči d At wul yeṣfan akkit.
Maca selmed-as daɣen belli ɣer tama n yal yir netta, yella lefḥel.
Selmed-as belli ɣer tama n bu yir tsertit, yella yimḍebbeṛ lɛali.
Selmed-as belli ɣer tama n yal aɛdaw, yella umdakkel.
Ḥsiɣ, annect-a ad yiḥwiǧ akud, maca selmed-as, ma tweɛɛaḍ, belli adulaṛ i d-iḥella s yiman-is yif xemsa i yufa.
Seḥfeḍ-as ad yissin d acu d anamek n lexṣaṛa, maca selmed-as ad yessibnen d acu i d anamek n rrbeḥ.
Beɛɛed-it ɣef tismin tisemmamin, ma tweɛɛaḍ, selmed-as sser n taḍsa n wul yennecṛaḥen.
Yessefk ad yissin si temẓi dakken d imjuṛen i iḥemmlen mliḥ asqizzeb.
Selmed-as, ma testufaḍ, ifeǧǧiǧen n yidlisen.
Maca efk-as cwiṭ n wakud i netta akken ad yettweḥḥed deg umkerwa war nnger n yigḍad deg tegnewt.

Tamurt taqbaylit tezga tettidir deg timanit ula deg tallit n umnekcam aṭurki deg Tefriqt n Ugafa.
Ankara tezga tferren mgal timunent n Zzayer deg Yiwanaken Yedduklen gar 1954 d 1962.
Mehenni yesbedd Amussu i Timanit n tmurt n Yiqbayliyen anida yuɣal d aselway n Unabaḍ Aqbayli Uɛḍil di lɣerba deg Fṛansa seg tallit n tefsut taberkant n tmurt n yiqbayliyen deg 2001, anida aɣref aqbayli yella yettqabal aseḥreṣ n Unabaḍ Azzayri mgal idles-is d tutlayt-is.
Tamurt n Yiqbayliyen tezga-d deg tama n ugafa n Zzayer, rrif n yilel Agrakal, tella tettidir deg timanit deg Tallit Talemmast akked wussan n umnekcam Aɛetman, sakin tuɣal tekcem deg Zzayer deg tallit n umnekcam Afṛansis deg tlemmast n lqern wis 19.
"Tamurt Taqbaylit tessefta deg timagit-is, maca urǧin tella d lqelɛa i tineslemt", i d-yenna Mehenni.

Ɛeddan ddeqs n wussan si Ṛemḍan armi qrib ad ifakk, nkemmel-iten akken nuɣ tanumi.
Tikwal nettenkar-d ɣer ṣḥuṛ, maca akken kan ad nečč neɣ ad nezhu.
Ulac seg-neɣ wid-nniden yettuzamen, ala baba akked yemma.
Armi d yiwen n wass seg wussan ineggura, iluɛa-yi-d baba yenna: Ma tebɣiḍ azekka uẓam azgen n wass.
Ad ttneggizeɣ si lfeṛḥ.
Nniɣ-as: A Ba, Meɛna ad aliɣ ɣe ssqef.
Dinna ara ččeɣ aḥbub!
Baba yecmumeḥ, yerra-yi-d: Ih a mmi.
Yerna ad tesweḍ aman di tbuqalt-nni n jida-k.
Lliɣ ad ttraǧuɣ ṣhuṛ.
Atmaten-iw d yisetma ggunan-iyi.
Iḍ kamel ur ṭṭiseɣ.
Armi qrib ad d-yaweḍ dɣa yewwi-iyi nnadam, ṭṭseɣ.
Baba d yemma ur yi-d-skiren ara.
Ihi azekkayen ṣbeḥ rfiɣ.
Yemma tenna: Ulac aɣilif a mmi.
Kemmel uẓam, mi telluẓeḍ ečč.
Rriɣ-as: Ur tetteɣ ara arma d tameddit.
Ihi, kemmelɣ akken taṣebḥit-nni Uẓameɣ.
Ttawiɣ, ttarreɣ seg uxxam ɣer tmazirt.
Dɣa mi yebda yettewwa lexirif, tikwal teffɣeɣ ad leqḍeɣ kra n yiniɣman.
Ttawiɣ-ten fettreɣ-ten deg uferrug aneggaru i yersen di tlemmast n tmazirt anida i nga ṭerḥa.
Akken yebda iḥemmu wass, fad yebda yettaɣ deg-i.
Teḍra yid-i am win i wumi ɛerqen lecɣal.
Ɣer uzal n wass, yeṭṭef-iyi fad yeskaw-iyi agerjum.
Deg uxxam ttṛumuqen-iyi-d, ladɣa ayetma d yisetma.
Ur zmireɣ ara ad sweɣ zdat-sen neɣ ma ulac ur ttaliɣ ara tameddit ɣer ssqef.
Ihi, ddmeɣ abelyun n waman, ččureɣ-t-id si tsebbalt.
Rniɣ wwiɣ yid-i sḍel n tissit swyes ara surgeɣ aman.
Ddiɣ ɣer uɛecciw akken ad muddeɣ aman i wakraren d tiyuzaḍ.
Aɛecciw tuɣ yebḍa ɣef sin.
Si tama d tiyuzaḍ, si tama-nniḍen d akraren.
Gar-asen, neẓḍa-asen aɣrab s uɣanim si ṭṭerf ɣer ṭṭerf.
Neǧǧa kan cwiṭ n tseɣlit akken ad nkeččem ɣer texxamt n yiyuẓaḍ, imi aɛecciw-nni yesɛa kan yiwet n tewwurt.
Deg ubrid-iw ɣer ixerfiyen, ɛeddeɣ ddaw n tbelɣenjuṛt i d-yezgan tama n tewwurt taxeṛṛaǧit si lḥaṛa ɣer tmazirt.
Kniɣ leqqḍeɣ-d kra n yiḥbuben.
Ḥusseɣ i wayetma ttsiggin-d seg uxxam, wa si ṭṭaq, wa si texnact, wa seg uṭeɛṭuj n lḥiḍ.
Lḥasun ẓriɣ ttɛassan-iyi-d.
Ihi, serseɣ abelyu-nni n waman akked sḍel-nni swayes i gliɣ.
Wwiɣ iniɣman-nni i d-leqḍeɣ serseɣ-iten deg uferrug akken i yi-d-walin.
Maca mi d-uɣaleɣ, zziɣ-d deffir n lḥiḍ n wadda n uɛecciw akken ur yi-d-ttwalin ara.
Tella dinna yiwet n tɣanimt.
Ṭinzeɣ leqḍeɣ-d kra n yiniɣman.
Rriɣ tlata ɣer lǧib s zreb, wiyaḍ wwiɣ-ten-id deg ufus-iw, briɣ-asen deg uferrug akken i yi-d-walin.
Uɣaleɣ-d, s abeylyun-nni refdeɣ-t, rriɣ daxel-is sḍel wwiɣ-ten ɣer uɛecciw.
Mi kecmeɣ, ẓiẓeɣ-d tawwurt-nni.
Surgeɣ aman i wakraren.
Ǧǧiɣ sin n sḍul i yiyuẓaḍ.
Mi kecmeɣ ɣer texxamt n yiyuzaḍ, uẓeɣ-d ɣer teɣmert idergen ugar.
Ddmeɣ-d sḍel, qelḥeɣ aman, rniɣ ččiɣ tlata-nni n yiniɣman.
Surgeɣ aman i d-yeqqimen ɣer lḥila-nsen n tisit sakin ffɣeɣ, zemmeɣ-d tiwwura uliɣ-d s axxam.
Akken i d-ḍilleɣ ɣer tewwurt n uxxam, yenna gma: Aqemmuc-ik d azeggaɣ!
Nniɣ-as: Ih, axaṭeṛ yeḥma lḥal d ibeṛṛa. Twalaḍ akka ad ttqudduṛeɣ d tidi?
Uletma terna-d: D aman ara tettquddureḍ mačči d tidi!
Suffeɣ-d kan iles-ik!
Dɣa suffɣeɣ-d iles-iw.
Walan qqimen-d kra n yibzizen deg uqemmuc-iw.
Lḥaṣun, ur i yi-ǧǧin kra.
Nekk ad asen-qqaṛeɣ uẓameɣ, nutni ṛwan taḍsa.
Maca zgiɣ nekkṛeɣ.
Ṣṣeḥ d baba akked yemma.
Ass kamel uɣaleɣ am ḥriṭa.
Ttawiɣ ttareɣ.
Tikwal ad ffɣeɣ ad leqḍeɣ iḥbuben s tuffra.
Kra s aqemmuc, kra ɣer uferrug.
Ass-nni, ixerfiyen d yiyuzaḍ ṛwan aman armi qrib ad tfakk tsebbalt.
Ar tmeddit n wass, mi yebda yiṭij iɣelli, baba ikcem-d.
Dɣa neṭṭḍeɣ ɣur-s.
Neffeɣ nettraǧu ad yedden ccix.
Baba mi d-yekcem, yella yewwi-d yid-s tini.
Ttraguɣ tuddna am waggur n lɛid.
Akken yedden, yessuli-yi baba ɣer ssqef.
Atmaten-iw d yisetma ttaḍsan.
Yemma ad ttɛeyyiḍ fell-asen ad susmen.
Maca nekk ur iyi-d-tewqiɛ ara deg-sen.
Yefka-yi-d baba aɛeqqa n ttmeṛ akked uḥbub ččiɣ-ten di sin.
Yerna-yi-d swiɣ aman di tbuqalt n jida.
Yemma tessiɣret, dɣa ffɣen-d lǧiran, walan-iyi-d akk di ssqef.
Nekk lliɣ ttafgeɣ si lferḥ.
Uɣaleɣ umneɣ am akken d tidet uẓameɣ.
Mi fukkeɣ, fkiɣ aqedmir n uḥbub, d yiɣes-nni n tini i yemma, rniɣ-as tabuqalt.
Teẓẓa-ten di tḥibus-nni nneɛneɛ.
Tenna-yi-d akken i as-tenna i gma ass-nni mi yuẓam.
Yessers-iyi-d baba.
Nkemmel nečča imensi lwaḥid.
Nesɛedda iḍ s tmucuha.
Maca seg wassen ur ssineɣ amek iga Ṛemḍan.
Sawleɣ-as yakan.
Yebzeg ucenfir-iw.
Wa Rabaḥ! Wa Rabah! Rǧu a ddin yemma-k!
Ah d nnuba-w ah!
Yeffuṛes Merzuq tagnit.
Ur ẓriɣ anida i lliɣ zhiɣ armi i yi-tṛuḥ nnuba-w.
Yuli ɣer tbeṛwiḍt, dɣa yennuheṛ-it Rabaḥ.
Rabaḥ yerra-d tiɣri s wadda: Ṛǧu ar d-uɣaleɣ ay imiɛruf.
Tura ad neɣleɣ Meṛzuq.
Imeddukal-iw imir-nni semman-iyi "Imiɛruf" acku taɣect-iw d taqesḥant.
Kra seg-sen regglen imeẓẓuɣen-nsen ticki ttiẓẓifeɣ.
Taberwiḍt-nni yettaǧa-tt-id Dda Ḥmed deg utemmu-is.
Daymi i tt-id-nettaddam.
Maca, lemmer ad d-iḍal fell-aɣ, ad tekker čaqlala gar-as d yimawlan-nneɣ.
Yesseqdac-itt mi ara d-yessalay isɣaren seg yiɣzeṛ.
Ugin-as lǧiran ad yesɛeddi zzayla-s, imi ṛebban-d akk tileqqamin.
Tikwal zzayla-s tettemmeɣ tettett tileqqamin-nni.
Ddeqs i tkerrec.
Dɣa rfan akk lǧiran-is.
Acḥal n tikkal ttberrin fell-as, armi dayen yeqqen zzayla-s deg n ugudu n udɣaɣ anida yeṭṭuqqet usennan n uɣyul.
Akken yewweḍ Rabaḥ s adda, yetti taberwiḍt, yenɣel Merẓuq.
Meṛzuq yeggrurej-d am tqejmuṛt.
Yetti snat n tikkal neɣ ahat tlata, dɣa yerked ɣer uɛemmuṛ n ufras yennewdemen ɣer lǧedra n txeṛṛubt.
A-t-a Ṛabaḥ yuɣal-d.
Ideggir-d di tbeṛwiḍt s lǧehd di tsawent-nni.
Tegguma ad tali imi teɛwej cwiṭ ṛṛuda-s.
Tama tazelmaḍt n tberwiḍt-nni tegzem.
Ticki yerkeb deg-s walbaɛḍ, tafekka-s akk ad tmal ɣer tama tayeffust.
Ilaq ad ickenṭeḍ deg-s win ara irekben akken ur iɣelli ara uqbel ad yaweḍ ɣer uqettun-nni n uhicuṛ i nesnewdem ɣer txeṛṛubt-nni i d-yezgan ɣer yiri n ucruf.
Win ur newwiḍ ara ɣer din, ad yexseṛ urar.
Ihi d netta ara d-yeḥwin akk lmal-nneɣ tameddit.
Beddeɣ-d si tiɣilt ad sikkideɣ di Rabaḥ ad d-yettali.
Ilehhet seg udegger di tbeṛwiḍt-nni i yegguman ad tali.
Tikwal, mi ara tewḥel kra deg uṛixsiw, ad yazzel wayeḍ ad tt-id-refden, ad tt-id-rren s abrid.
Rabaḥ d netta i d ameqqran akk deg-neɣ, daymi i t-nerra d anehhaṛ.
Akken i d-yewweḍ ɣer tqaɛet n tiɣilt, heggeɣ iman-is ad aliɣ.
Dɣa yenṭeq-d: Ṛǧu ad steɛfuɣ ciṭ ay imiɛruf.
Iẓẓan, i as-rriɣ.
Rniɣ-as: Ur ttuɣal ara ad yi-d-tessiwleḍ akka.
Isem-iw Muḥ, yak! I as-rniɣ.
Akken i tekkaw tidi-s.
Yerra-d nnehta, Rabaḥ yenna: Ali tura.
Uliɣ, srekdeɣ iman-iw.
Arrac meṛṛa bedden-d di tiɣilt, ttraǧun.
Ssaramen akk ad ɣliɣ uqbel ad awḍeɣ ɣer yiḍumman-nni.
Ckenteḍeɣ s yifasen-iw ɣer yiri tberwiḍt.
Rabaḥ iṛeqraq-d di tkessert-nni am lebreq.
Akken yezgen umecwaṛ, ṛṛuda teffeɣ abrid.
Tewwet di tderrit dɣa tufeg tberwiḍt tuli deg yigenni.
Nekk nnḍeɣ iman-iw am uqenfud.
Aqeṛṛu-w gar tgejrar ɣer tama n yifassen-iw am takurt.
Maca, mačči d kra ara ṣebreɣ.
Ḥulfeɣ i yiffasen-iw ttaqṛaḥen.
Cellḥen seg yiri-nni n tbeṛwiḍt Dɣa ḍelqeɣ-asen.
Zelliɣ-d si tberwiḍt am ticict.
Berrneɣ snat n tikkal deg yigenni.
Taberwiḍt terra ɣer tama tazelmaḍt, nekk rriɣ s ayeffus.
Ɣliɣ-d ɣer ẓẓerb n tmazirt n Ḥemmu.
wwteɣ axenfuc-iw ɣer usɣar n tmidekt.
Neṭḍeɣ din ad tɣileḍ d llazuq i as-rran.
Cwi kan ur d-ɣliɣ ara ɣef tzeggart-nni yellan ddaw-as.
Tili ulac anawa ad yid-yekksen.
Taberwiḍt mi tewwet di ẓẓerb n tmazirt n Si Bṛahim, tɛawed tuɣal-d dɣa tett-id, tennewdam-d fell-i, tḥeṛṛ-iyi ddaw-as.
Arrac s ufella rwan akeḥkeḥ.
Nekk kmumseɣ deg umkan am taduṭ, ur zmireɣ ad ḥerkeɣ.
Dɣa udren-d.
Meqran d Maǧid refden-d taberwiḍt.
Farid yefsiyi-id am akken fettin takemmust.
Iḍal ɣer yifassen-iw yufa-ten xebcen cwiṭ maca acenfir-iw icelleḥ.
Yuzzel yekkes-d ḥlafa.
Iḥukk-itt deg yifassen-is armi i d-tserreḥ i waman, sakin yebda iteẓẓem-itt-id ɣef ucelliḥ-nni i mazal iḍeggir-d idammen.
Ɣer taggara, isenned-d ḥlafa-nni i d-yeggran ɣef ucenfir-iw, dɣa yenna: Ṭṭef-itt s ufus-ik ar d-tekkaw ay imiɛruf.
Rfiɣ, bɣiɣ ad d-bbaɛezqeɣ.
Imi yettaqṛaḥ uqemmuc-iw, ur zmireɣ ara ad d-mmeslayeɣ akken ilaq.
Ur uksaneɣ ara. Afus-iw ɣef tfidi n uncenfir, nekk ttuṛṛakeɣ: Inɛel ddin n ubabat n baba-k.
Arrac ṛwan tadṣa.
Dɣa yenṭeq-d Maǧid: Ass-a d nnuba-k ad teḥwiḍ lmal.
Kker tura beṛka-k asteɛmel.
Ulac d acu i k-yuɣen.
Snewdameɣ-d, seggmeɣ-d iman-iw.
Qqumceɣ, tekkeɣ azagur-iw ɣer usɣar-nni n tmidekt.
Arrac zzin-d akk ad ttqeṣṣiren.
Ma d nekk tafekka-aw meṛṛa tessebraq.
Ibda iɣelli-d yiḍ.
Aqraḥ ad yettenɣas.
Rriɣ-d d akesser ɣer teẓgi ad d-saliɣ lmal imi xeṣreɣ urar.
Di tiɣilt mi d-uɣaleɣ, yal wa yefra akraren-is inuheṛ-iten.
Nnekk friɣ-d ayla-w rriɣ-d s axxam.
Mi wwḍeɣ, yemma twala lǧerḥ-nni deg ucenfir akked yixebbicen deg yifassen.
Testeqsa-yi-d, nniɣ-as: D tiderrit i yi-yewwten deg ubrid a Yyi.
Terra-yi-d: Ɣellin akk wararc a mmi.
Akka i d-yeǧǧa Ṛebbi ddunit.
Tuɣ iḍ-nni, zegleɣ imensi imi ur zmireɣ ara ad greɣ lqut s aqemmuc-iw.
Ihi tekker yemma tseww-d taḥelwiḍt n uwren.
Terra-as cwiṭ n zzit n uzemmur, ṭṭseɣ akken.
Azekkayen ṣṣbeḥ mi d-kkreɣ, acenfir-iw yebzeg.
Iɛleq-d d akesser am ucenfir n ulɣem.
Acḥal d ussan ṛwan warrac deg-i taḍsa.
Mmi-s n Quḥḥu isečč abquq i mmi-s n xalti-s.
Aql-aɣ di tazwara n tefsut n useggas n 1983.
D aseggas wis 3 n deg uɣerbaz amezwaru deg Uzemmur Umeryem.
Tfukk tegrest, ideflawen fsin.
Lḥammu tebda tettali, ijeggigen fsan.
Tamurt teṭṭerḍeq d tudert.
Ifrax deg yigenni ttɣennin, iɣersiwen imalayen saḥen ɣef tuntiyin.
Ula d aɣyul-nni n Quḥḥu isaḥ, d aɣyul maca d amcum.
Ttsetḥin ula d imdanen ad d-ɛeddin tama anida i t-itteqqen bab-is.
Ur tẓriḍ d acu ara yexdem.
Tuɣ ttasen-d waɛraben, ttawin-d lmal, gellun-d s tiɣyal.
Kerrun iɛerqyab ticki ifukk warwat.
Maca mazal lḥal akka tura.
Aɣyul ameɣbun mazal-t ihaj.
Idurar d yizuɣar i d-yezzin i taddart, uɣen akk udem n tizegzewt, tewreɣ d tezweɣ n yijeggigen.
D lǧennet yettfeggiḍen d tudert d lferḥ di yal tama.
Di tefsut, nettaf iman-nneɣ s uɣẓaẓ: tuɣmest n temɣart d yimemmuyen-is, sseɣdeṛ d teɣma si yal ṣṣifa.
Lḥasun ulac aɣeddiw ur nečči.
Tameddit ticki nekcem-d s axxam ama seg uɣerbaz neɣ seg teksawt, nettɛebbi-d d imeqqunen n yimɣan am bibras, tarnest, wahṛar, tasulla neɣ tansawt.
Meqqeṛ ad nesteɛfu cwiṭ si lebqel-nni n lleft itteffuḥun.
Ḥsen mmi-s n Quḥḥu d zzlamiṭ.
Urǧin yessen d acu d rrekdan.
Ad yili yeqqim tama-k, maca mi d-trefdeḍ allen-ik, igenni ur yeddim, tamurt ur tsebleɛ.
Mi tsakdeḍ, ad tafed-t yejjeɛluleq ɣer tzemmurt neɣ ad d-yezzuɣuṛ albaɛḍ n yiɣerwas.
Tikwal daɣen arma yuɣal-d kan s lɛec d yigḍaḍ ileqqaqen gar yifassen-is.
D imsefsed.
Lḥasun am cciṭan.
Ula deg uɣebaz, iselmaden ḥaren amek ara s-xedmen.
Aḥrac yeḥrec, maca ur yessin ad yessers tazagurt-is xarsum kra n lweqt.
Tikkelt, Ḥsen yewwi-d yid-s mmi-s xalti-s Saɛid Ameẓyan ɣer Tilas anida nuɣ tanumi nkes.
Maca ass-nni, neffeɣ kan ad nmerreḥ cwiṭ.
Saɛid meẓẓi, mazal-t d aleqqaq.
Yella yettidir di Zzayer.
Di lawan-nni mazal-t ur yekcim ara s aɣerbaz.
Yerna mi t-nessenqed, nufa-t ur yedhiṛ ara ɛad.
Ad nteddu gar yizemran, dɣa newweḍ ɣer yiwen n umḍiq yeččuṛ d abquq.
Nekk lhiɣ-d ad tekkseɣ ijeggigen n cciḥbuḍ.
Sliɣ-as i Saɛid ad as-yeqqaṛ i Ḥsen: D acu-t wagi a Dadda?
Ḥsen yerra-as: wagi d claḍa a Saɛid.
Nekk ḍsiɣ-d akken cwiṭ makken ad s-yesmejgir Ḥsen i Saɛid.
Ihi uɣaleɣ-d ad meggreɣ ijeggigen n cciḥbuḍ.
Armi sliɣ kan i leɛyaḍ.
Dɣa uzzleɣ-d
Ufiɣ Saɛid yeɣli di tmurt, yettexbibiḍ, yettaṭṭaf teɛbbuḍt-is, ur ẓriɣ d acu yeḍran.
Acu-t akka, acu-t akka? I a-snniɣ i Ḥsen.
Yenṭeq-d Ḥsen, yenna: Yečča abquq.
Azzel, azzel wali ma tella Nna Taseɛdit, tmeṭṭut n Dda Lmulud, di tmazirt-is. Wali ma tesɛa zzit uzemmur.
I as-nniɣ i Ḥsen zzalamiṭ.
Ḥsen yerra-d d asawen, nekk refdeɣ-d Ṣaɛid ḍefreɣ-t-id.
Maca ẓẓay, sakin ḥebseɣ.
Werdin kan a-t-a yuɣal-d Ḥsen, tedda-d yid-s yid-s Nna Taseɛdit.
Tewwi-d gar ifassen-is tasupirt n zzit.
Di lawan-nni, imdanen ticki ddan ɣer tmizar, aɛwin-nsen d zzit, d iḥbuben, d aman, akked uɣrum n temẓin.
Tikwal ttawin daɣen iɣi.
Akken i d-tewweḍ Nna Taseɛdit, serseɣ-d Saɛid ɣef uɛrur-iw, teldi-as aqemmuc-is, tesseblaɛ-as zzit s uḥettem.
Saɛid yettiẓẓif̣, yettru.
Yerra-d akk ayen yessebleɛ.
Yeqqim, itekka ɣef yijifaṛ n tmeṭṭut n Dda Lmulud.
Kra n lweqt kan yekker.
Dɣa nerra-d d asawen.
Maca lliɣ rfiɣ.
Ad ttiwzageɣ.
Mi i d-newweḍ ɣer terga Lḥaǧ Ɛli, tama anida yezdeɣ Ḥsen, azegḍuf yeheṛfel, ad yeqqaṛ d nekk i d nekk.
Ul-iw yeqbeṛ si reffu seg wayen yexdem Ḥsen i mmi-s n xalti-s.
Mmɣeɣ kkseɣ-d tameqqunt n uzegḍud, ḥukkeɣ-as-t i Ḥsen ɣef wudem-is armi ur yezmir ad iwali tigert.
Seg uqraḥ-nni, yerwel ur yeẓri anida ara iger iḍarren-is, dɣa yenfel ddaw ubrid.
Yecceḍ yegrireb d akesser armi i t-id-teḥbes tnijjelt.
Lḥasun yexbec seg yiḍarren armi d aqeṛṛu.
Neǧǧa-t dinna, nkemmel-d abrid akked Saɛid.
Ṭṭfeɣ afus i Saɛid, wwiɣ-t-id s axxam n Quḥḥu, argaz n xalti-s.
Akken i aɣ-d-ldin tawwurt, nekcem ɣer lḥaṛa, nufa Ḥsen ɣef lmida ay itess lqahwa ntmeddit akked baba-s.
Yenṭeq-d s ucmumeḥ ɣef wudem-is, yenna: Zwareɣ-ken-id! zwareɣ-ken-id!
Dda Ḥmimic, sḍis n tmerwin d semmus n iseggasen aya i yettidir deg taddart-is deg Sidi Ɛic.

Tislit-is qarren-as Tafrara.
Ass mi i d-tewweḍ Tafrara s axxam, tegdeh aṭas imi ula d yiwen deg uxxam n urgaz-is ur yeqqin ɣer uẓeṭṭa Internet.
Nettat teɣra taneflit Web.
Ddeqs i tesnefli n yifecka Web s useqdec n tetiknulijiyin Web am HTML, CSS akked JavaScript.
Yerna daɣen tessen ula d Python, yiwet n tutlayt n usihel i yettuseqdacen s waṭas iseggasen-agi ineggura.
Wagi dayen tessen Tafrara deg akud-nni, semmus n yiseggasen aya. Ass-a d ayen-nniḍen.
Tafrara twala d akken imdanen n taddart ur ssinen ara taqbaylit tatrart.

Tafrara tuɣal d tanedbalt n tutlayt taqbaylit deg ddeqs n yisenfaṛen deg Web.
Tessuqul, tessidig s tutlayt-is taqbaylit.
Tafrara tseqdac ddeqs n wanawen n yifecka n tsuqilt, amad d ifecka inmeggagen n tsuqilt srid deg Web, neɣ ifecka idiganen.

Tafrara tefren kra n yisnasen.
Di tazwara, tenna ttif xir limer ad nheggi ifecka i seqdacen tuget n yimdanen am iẓeḍwa inmettiyen, ifecka n usefrek n yiznan, ifecka n tunigin, ifecka n usefrek n yiḍrisen, akked yifecka n usefrek n tizmilin.

Nessuffeɣ-it ɣer berra ɣer targa rrif n lḥedd n ccix Saɛid.
Nessa di tazwara aɣanim-nni sakin neburr-as ahicuṛ i d-nejmeɛ.
Nerra taseɣlit akken tella, sakin neṭṭef-d abrid d asawen.
Azekkayen tameddit armi nesla kan ccix Saɛid uzlig yeɣli deg-s yeṛṛeẓ deg ufus.
Taddart meṛṛa tɣil d awqaɛ i yuqeɛ deg tesraft i ttandin yilmeẓyen i yilfan.
Meɛna nekni neẓra.
Di tazwara, nethenna kra n wussan seg-s.
Maca mi tɛedda tallit-nni, iɣaḍ-aɣ meskin.
Ṛebbi ur as-d-yefka, nekni nkemmel-as.
Ad aɣ-isemmeḥ kan.
Deg unebdu n 1990, tuɣ mazal-iyi deg uɣerbaz alemmas ,maca nella deg yimuṛas.
Nella nettheggi tuɣalin ɣer useggaz aneggaru anida i aɣ-yettṛaǧu ugerdas n taggara.
Imuṛas-nneɣ ur cbin wid n yilmeẓyen-nniḍen deg umaḍal, imi ahil-nneɣ iban.
Tasebḥit nettenkar zik, nberru i lmal.
Ticki yuli-d yiṭij, ad d-nenheṛ.
Deffir n yimekli, ad nemlil d tarbaɛt, ad nerr akin s asif anida i nesɛedday lweqt deg ucucef di tmedwin, takerḍa n tẓidanin si tmizar, akked wurar.
Tameddit, ad d-nekcem s axxam ad nebru daɣen i lmal.
D taksawt, d urar, d ččaqlala akken arma yeɣli-d yiḍ.
Tuget deffir n yimensi, nteffeɣ-d ɣer umṛaḥ n taddart, ad d-nessu aslen neɣ kalitus akken arma yezgen yiḍ.
Tikwal, nettkemmil din iḍes arma d ṣṣbeḥ.
Imawlan-nneɣ tteklen, ẓran ulac cwal neɣ tiwaɣiyin.
Di lawan-nni ula d abrid yettṛebi.
Ulac win ara yettɛeddin ɣef wayeḍ.
Yella leqdeṛ, yella uḥezzeb ama ɣer warrac neɣ ɣer yimawlan.
Deg yiwen n wass deg ussan n Ṛebbi deg waggur n Ctember n 1990, neṭṭef abrid s asif akken kan yezgen wass.
Ass-nni tella d tiɣli.
Tuɣ kra n wussan uqbel, ɣlin-d waman.
Ifellaḥen kkren i tyerza, irgazen d tlawin bdan afras n tmizar d yizemran.
Ihi nufa deg ubrid-nneɣ deg yiwen n uḥriq, Dda Ḥmed d tyuga-s.
Dda Ḥmed d akerraz.
Yes-sen i ikerrez timizar akked iḥerqan, acku ulac allalen atraren imiren-nni deg taddart.
Neɣ xas ma llan, mačči d ayen i yezmer ad yesseqdec umdan deg yikerkiren am wid-nni.
Akal yezleg, yemmal, ur yewsiɛ ara akken ad tizmir tmacint ad tɛeddi dinna.
Dda ḥmed iḥemmel abucun, nekkni neẓra.
Nluɛa-t: Axiṛ a Dda Ḥmed! Ad iɛin Ṛebbi.
Dda Ḥmed iwala-aɣ-d, yesseḥbes tayuga-is.
Irfed-d aqeṛṛu-s, sakin yerra-d: Axiṛ lɛafya a tarwa! Anida akka ara tetteddum ay arrac?
Ɣer wasif, a Dda Ḥmed, i as-nerra.
Maca, tura semmeḍ lḥal a tarwa.
Ɣur-wat ad taḍnem, i aɣ-d-yerra.
Rnu ɣur-s, asif yewwi-d aluḍ d usɣar deg uḥemmal n wussan-a, ihi ɣur-wat! Ttḥadaret!
Anɛam a Dda Ḥmed.
Awah! neẓra.
Ma ɣumment tmedwin, ur neccecuf ara, i as-nerra.
Ihi, nkemmel-d abrid.
Akken nḍal deffir n lekdeṛ yettawin s asif, nezzi-d s wadda, nuɣal-d armi d anida i ikerrez Dda Ḥmed.
Neffer-d deg teẓgi n yinijjel i d-yezzin i uḥriq-nni seg yidis n wadda, dɣa neqqim nessikid-d ɣer Dda Ḥmed d acu i la ixeddem.
Lḥasun ur zmireɣ ara ad d-ḥkuɣ sekra n wayen nwala.
Maca yiwet ad tt-id-iniɣ.
Nṛumeq Dda ḥmed ticki yewwi adur arma d talast tayeffust, ad yeddu ɣer yiwen n ukerra, ad yeddem taqreɛt n ccrab ad yessew tiqqit.
Sakin ad tt-yessers ddaw n ukerra.
Ad d-yuɣal ad d-yawi adur-nniḍen ɣer tama tazelmaḍt.
Mi yewweḍ ɣer ṭṭerf, ad yesseḥbes daɣen izeggaren-is, ad yemmeɣ ddaw n ukerra ad d-yeddem taqerɛet tis snat, ad yessew tiqqit, sakin ad tt-yerr ddaw ukerra.
Mi yewwi adur, ad yessew tiqqit, mi d-yuɣal ad yernu tayeḍ.
Akken kan i tt-yettawi arma fukkent snat n tqerɛunin.
Sakin ad yemmeɣ ɣer tneqqalin n zzayla-is i yessers rrif n lǧedra n tzemmurt, ad d-yeddem daɣen snat-nniḍen ad ten-yessers ta deg uyeffus, ta deg uzelmaḍ.
Tuɣ zzayla-is yeqqen-itt-id kan nnig-nneɣ, ad tkes rrif n tnijjelt anida nella neffer.
Ihi, uliɣ-d cwiṭ ɣer tama tayeffust deffir n tnijjelt imi llant dinna kra n tzemrin ur frisent ara.
Tella cwiṭ n teɛfeṛt akked usaɣur ur nḥucc ara.
Mmurdeɣ ɣef tgejrar d yifassen d asawen.
Ihuza-yi-d cwiṭ n ubenqaṛ deg yifassen-iw akked yisennanen n uɣyul deg uḍar-iw.
Akken wwḍeɣ ɣer tzemmurt rrif n talast, ffreɣ daxel n wuruz, sikideɣ-d Dda Ḥmed.
Dda Ḥmed yuɣ agudi s azelmaḍ.
Nekk qurɛeɣ-t-id.
Ẓerb tuɣ ulac.
Tilas di lawan-nni d tikfillin kan.
Ihi qqimeɣ cwiṭ dinna acku Dda Ḥmed qrib ad yaweḍ ɣer talast tazelmaḍt.
Ugadeɣ ma yezzi-d ad iyi-d-iwali.
Ihi Ṛǧiɣ-t armi i d-yuɣal.
Akken yeswa tiqqit tayeffust, yeṭṭef abrid yuɣal s azelmaḍ.
Di lawan mi yezgen adur, ffɣeɣ-d seg uruz, ddiɣ ɣer ukerra, swiɣ s zreb, erriɣ tabutayt ddaw n ukerra, sakin rewleɣ-d ɣer wuruz.
Imeddukal-iw, llan ttɛassan-d mebɛid.
Dɣa ulin-d ula d nitni s ttawil.
Neṛǧa daɣen Dda Ḥmed armi yewwi adur s azelmad, dɣa mmɣen sin-nniḍen ddmen-d taqerɛunt wwten yal yiwen seg-sen tiqqit-is.
Rran taqerɛunt s amkan-is.
Akken-nni kan armi neswa i xemsa seg-neɣ.
Tikkelt mi d-yuɣal Dda Ḥmed, yeddem-d taqerɛunt-nni, ad tt-yessikid.
Ikemmez s uḍad-is tamart-is am akken ikcem-it ccek.
Yeswa, yessers taqerɛunt-nni.
Mi yewweḍ ɣer tama tazelmaḍt, yeddem-d taqerɛunt-nni-nniḍen, yessikid-itt daɣen uqbel ad yessew.
Nekni nugad, nenna-as ad nernu kan tajɣimt tajɣimt i yiwen, sakin ad nkemmel abrid s asif.
Neṛǧa armi i tfukk tbutayt-nni.
Dda Ḥmed yeddem-d tayeḍ yessers-itt deffir n ukerra.
Tuɣ netta aqerru-s yeḥma, ihi yuɣal ula d adur yettawi-as ugar n lweqt.
Yettɛeṭṭil deg-s.
Nfuṛes tagnit mi yewwi adur ɣer tama tazelmaḍt, neffeɣ-d di xemsa, neddem-d taqerɛunt neqleh-itt akken s zreb armi tezgen.
Dɣa nesser-itt, maca ur tt-nerri ara ddaw n ukerra.
Sakin neṭṭef-d abrid ɣer wasif mebla ma iwala-aɣ-d Dda Ḥmed.
Akken, kan nger kra n yisurifen, armi nesla i Dda Ḥmed yettɛeggiḍ: Ay arraw n taǧǧalt!
Lɛerbi amucaṛ yunda cmingu i Si Yidir.
Si Yidir yezga yettuṛṛak.
Nsemma-as tiẓirna.
Akken i d-newweḍ si lexla, yemma tessers aqecwal-is n uzemmur.
Uzzleɣ wwiɣ amextaf-nni ad t-ɛellqeɣ ɣer tgejdit n uɛecciw.
Mi d-uɣaleɣ wwiɣ-d yid-i tacekkaṛt.
Ldiɣ-as imi-s, yemma tessureg azemmur-nni sakin nessewdem-itt ɣer lḥiḍ.
Kra n wakud kan yekcem-d baba s tezdemt n tleẓẓawt.
Yedda-d yid-s gma, yewwi-d taqabact n leqdiɛ akked tmeẓbert.
Yessers-iten tama n umextaf.
Baba iḥemmel ad yeqqim ɣer yiri n lkanun di ccetwa ladɣa ma d-teɣli tegrest.
Ticki yuɣal-d si tẓallit n lɛica, ad neqqim akk akken tama n lkanun ad d-nesseknaf baṭaṭa.
Tikwal nettawi-d tigreslin.
Ma d iɛuras yettagi.
Ihi nteffer-iten arma yedda ad yeṭṭes, sakin ad ten-id-nezzu.
Mi ara d-yaweḍ baba, ad yessired ad iẓal lmeɣreb, sakin ad aɣ-yawi yid-s ɣer lǧameɛ.
Di Lǧameɛ neqqaṛ Leqran.
Ddeqs n warrac i yettilin di lǧameɛ acku ulac anida ara ddun.
Mi ara nfakk neɣra-d Ḥizb Ɛemma d win akken i d-yernan deffir-s, Si Muḥ Lḥaǧ u Ceɛban, ccix n lǧameɛ, ad aɣ-d-imudd idrimen ad d-naɣ ccikula akked teḥlawatin.
D ayen i aɣ-yettawin ɣer lǧameɛ imir-nni.
Wama, ahbuh! Amzun di tmeqbert ay nella.
Ulac taḍsa, ulac zzhu.
Irgazen meqqren ttɣimin di beṛṛa.
Ad ttraǧun ar d-yaweḍ lweqt n tẓallit n Lɛica.
Mi nekfa nečča ccikula d tzidanin-nniḍen, ad d-nemdel tawwurt akken ad nurar tiqqaṛ daxel n lǧameɛ.
Lḥasun, acḥal d ussan neṭṭaqay ad nṛuḥ ɣer lǧameɛ ala ɣef teḥlawatin d tiqqaṛ.
Maca yewweḍ-d wass aneggaru.
Lɛerbi amucaṛ d agrud yeɛzel iman-is.
Nsemma-as amucaṛ acku yettawi tiɛlumin.
Yerna yettɛawad i yiselmaden-nneɣ akked imawlan-nneɣ ticki nexdem taɛewriḍt.
Mi ara aɣ-d-iwali nteddu lwaḥid d yigerdan-nniḍen, yettɣaḍ-it lḥal.
Iɣil am akken d nekkni i t-iɛezlen.
Lɛerbi yesɛedday tuget n lweqt-is deg uxxam n xali-s.
Netta mačči n taddart-nneɣ.
Dɣa mi yuɣ tanumi dinna, yeqqim.
Ijerred-it xali-s, yekcem-d ad iɣer yid-neɣ deg uɣerbaz-nneɣ.
Maca, d lmuṣiba.
Yiwen n wass deg iḍ, akken kan nfukk taɣuri n Ḥizb Ɛemma, Lḥaǧǧ imudd-aɣ-d idrimen.
Nuzzel ɣer Rruji nuɣ-d cikkula d teḥlawatin.
Akken i d-neffeɣ si tewwurt n tḥanut, nemmuger-d Lɛerbi amucaṛ.
Fket-iyi-d taḥeǧǧurt n ccikula, i d-yenna.
Yerna amzun d lameṛ.
Yerra-as meqqran: Ad teččeḍ iẓẓan.
A meqqran! Mudd-as yiwet seg wayla-w: I as-nniɣ.
Yenṭeq-d Meqqran: Teslam ihi! A-t-an ad as-fkeɣ yiwet n tḥeǧǧurt seg umur n Muḥ.
Ih! nesla, i d-rran meṛṛa warrac-nni.
Yefka-as meqqran taḥeǧǧurt n ccikula i Lɛerbi amucaṛ.
Nuɣal-d ɣer Lǧameɛ. Nufa-d dinna irgazen-nniḍen deg yibernyas-nsen.
Qqimen ɣef ugadir zdat lǧameɛ.
Tekkan ɣer lḥiḍ.
Lɛerbi d uccen.
Yeḥfeḍ Salam Ɛlikum.
Imɣaren-nni ḥesben-t d uḥdiq.
Dɣa, isellem fell-asen.
Ma d nekni nḍaq ad d-nekcem ɣer lǧameɛ, ad d-nemdel tawwurt, ad nečč, ad nurrar tiqqaṛ.
Nečča nekfa.
Agens n lǧameɛ yessa d iɛlawen.
Ɣas ma teɣliḍ, ur k-yettaɣ kra.
Dɣa nekkeṛ ɣer tiqqaṛ.
Lɛerbi amucaṛ, tameẓẓuɣt ɣer yimɣaren, tayeḍ ɣer daxel n lǧameɛ.
Ihi yesla-d i dderz n yiḍaṛṛen dɣa yeldi-d tawwurt yufa-aɣ-d wa yeɣli, wa yettneggiz, wa yekkat s rrkel.
Dɣa yezzi ɣer yimɣaren: A-ten-an ad tturaren aqeddami daxel n lǧameɛ.
Teṭṭeɛwec-d tẓirna, tettɛeggiḍ ɣef yimawlan-nneɣ yellan dinna: I tura kenwi ur tettsetḥim ara?
Ɣer lǧameɛ ad d-tettawim dderya-nwen?
Wagi d amkan n yirgazen.
Ur nqudeṛ ara axxam n Ṛebbi.
Ad nawi ddeɛwessu.
Annaɣ a Jeddi Mensuṛ!
Ad d-iḥeddeṛ Ṛebbi leɛna-ak, sellkeɣ si lqum n teǧǧal.
Nekni tuɣ neḥbes tiqqaṛ imir imir.
Nṣeggem iɛlawen.
Yal wa yuɣ tiɣmert di lǧameɛ amzun ur ḍrint.
Yenṭeq-d ɣur-s Lḥaǧ yenna-as: A si Yidir!
Wigi d ixulaf-nneɣ.
Axir ad qqimen da, wala ad ṛuḥen ɣer wanda-nniḍen.
D arrac, ad uraren.
Tuɣ nekk siggeɣ-d si tewwurt ad ttwaliɣ d acu ara yeḍerrun.
Ugadeɣ ad nawi taḍriḥt.
I wagi? Mačči d agrud? i as-d-terra tẓirna.
Netta yettwehhi ɣer Lɛerbi amucaṛ.
Yeslufu-as di tqerrut-is.
Dɣa, Lɛerbi amucaṛ iquffi, tettcuffu tserwalt-is.
Nekk ad t-smuqquleɣ, netta ad yi-d-yesmuqqul, amzun akken yebɣa ad d-yini "cceh".
Sweɛdeɣ-as-d s xemsa n yiḍudan n ufus akken ad yefhem d akken yella wayen ara t-yettraǧun.
A Dda Sli, a-t-an ad yettgalla deg-i, i as-yenna Lɛerbi i baba.
Baba yekker-d.
Ur yi-d-iwala ara beddeɣ ɣef umnar n tewwurt.
Nekk rewleɣ daxel n lǧameɛ.
Ṭṭfeɣ taṛkent.
Dɣa yenṭeq-d Muqqran: Rwu tura kečč i as-yefkan taḥeǧǧurt n ccikula.
Baba yeldi-d tawwurt, yessawel-iyi-d: Yya-n san!
Ffɣeɣ-d, dɣa yenna: Ad tettgallaḍ deg-s?
Ala a Ba, yerna fkiɣ-as taḥeǧǧurt n ccikula, i as-nniɣ.
Ma yella ur tumineḍ ara steqsi arrac-a, i as-rniɣ.
Arrac meṛṛa neṭqen-d: Ih a Dda Sli, yefka-as ccikula.
Ɣur-wat ad tennaɣem, yah! i d-yenna baba.
Ih a Ba! ih a Ba! i s-rriɣ.
Uɣaleɣ-d kecmeɣ-d ɣer lǧameɛ.
Jemɛeɣ-d akk cmingu-nni i nfeẓ.
Xedmeɣ-d takurt.
Ǧǧiɣ-tt deg ufus-iw.
Nniɣ-asen: Ṛgut kan ihi ad twalim.
Werdin kan yedden ccix.
Dɣa kecmen-d yirgazen-nni ɣer lǧameɛ.
Yekker Lḥaǧ yezwer ɣer Lmenbeṛ.
Adur amenzu bedden deg-s yirgazen, ɣer deffir d nekkni.
Lɛerbi amucaṛ yeḥnunez ad yeddu deg udur amezwaru maca ḥwin-t-id yemɣaren ɣer deffir.
Nekni neṛwa taḍsa.
Tebda tẓallit, nekk ṭṭṛaǧuɣ lawan n useǧǧed.
Akken seǧǧden, serseɣ ameqqun-nni n cmingu deg umkan anida yesrusu Si Yidir tazagurt-is.
Akken i d-yuɣal seg useǧǧed, yeqqim fell-as.
Yenṭeḍ uqenduṛ-is ɣer waɛlaw.
Mi d-kkren ad alsen i ṛṛekɛa, yekker-d Si Yidir dɣa yedda-d waɛlaw-nni.
Nekkni s deffir neṭṭerḍeq d taḍsa.
Ɣas wama di tlemmast i d-teḍra, Tiẓirna teǧǧa taẓallit.
Izzi-d ɣer deffir, yeggelfeɛ-d: A yir dderya!
Yemmeɣ yeddem-d afus n ubali i yersen din yessuffeɣ-aɣ-d meṛṛa.
Yegla ula s Lɛerbi amucaṛ yedda.
Mi d-wwḍeɣ s axxam, yemma tenna: Anida-t baba-k?
Nniɣ-as: Mazal-it yettẓala?
I kečč anida teddiḍ?
Mačči yid-s i telliḍ? i d-terna.
Ala, din i lliɣ, maca yeḥwi-aɣ-d Si Yidir, i as-nniɣ.
Emm! Ahat yella wayen i t-xedmeḍ.
Ur cukkeɣ ara ad ken-id-ḥwin kan akka, i d-terna.
Uzzleɣ s usu s zreb uqbel ad d-yaweḍ baba.
Akken sburreɣ taḥayekt,a-t-a yewweḍ-d.
Anida-t ubandi-nni?
Yemma tenna: Yeṭṭes.
Anef-as ihi ar ṣṣbeḥ, i as-dyerra baba.
Maca ssbeḥ d abrid ɣer uɣerbaz.
Ihi, am win yewwten nneḥ.
Ur teddiz ur tebriz.
Maca, seg wass-nni ur nezzi nuɣal ɣer Lǧameɛ.
Zik, tawsa tella amzun d lfetṛa ara nsuffeɣ.
D ayen terra tmetti d lwaǧeb deg tallit-nni.
Yal mi ara tili tmeɣra anida i nettwaɛraḍ, yessefk inebgawen ad mudden tawsa.
Yerna, ismawen n yimdanen d wazal n tewsa ad ttwajerden ɣef yimedlis i d-yettwaheggan i wanect-nni.
Nḥemmel timeɣriwin.
Acku si tama yettili ṭṭbel d ccḍeḥ ladɣa iḍebbalen.
Si tama tayeḍ, d tagnit akken ad nečč tacriḥt n uksum akked tsegrit ẓiden am waḍil, delleɛ, abeqqus, afettix, tteffaḥ, ifires neɣ ayen-nniḍen.
Lbanan deg tallit-nni ur tettaken ara deg tmeɣriwin, acku ulac-it neɣ ma yella ɣlay aṭas.
Tikwal daɣen, tasegrit d taqerɛunt n lgazuz.
Yerna ay alxiṛ ticki mudden-tt-id d tasemmaḍ deg unebdu qessiḥen n tuddar-nneɣ.
Nekker-d deg yiwet n twennaḍt tadelsant i yefkan aẓaṛ lqayen deg umezruy n tmetti taqbaylit.
Ɣer tama n temɛayin d tmucuha i aɣ-d-ḥekkun deg uxxam, ladɣa di tegrest ticki nezzi-d i lkanun, nsell daɣen i teḥkayin-nniden di beṛṛa i itezzin ɣef Waɣzen, Akli n Uzal, Anza, Buberrak, iɛessasen, leǧnun.
Lḥasun d rrebrab mgal arrac lemmer teqqim akken teswiɛt.
Nuɣal nettaggad azal, nettaggad iḍ, nettaggad tiqerrabin, iɛessasen, timqebrin, nettaggad ad nelḥu weḥd-neɣ deg yimeḍqan neɣ tignatin anida irennu lweḥc.
Yiwet n tikkelt, nella nettwaɛreḍ ɣer tmeɣra deg taddart deg udrar.
Ahat ad yili ɣur-is 8 neɣ 9 n yiseggasen kan.
Nekni tuɣ nezdeɣ deg tadddar deg uẓaɣar.
Imi nettwaɛreḍ ɣer yimensi, ilaq yiwen seg-neɣ ad yali ad yečč imensi, yerna ad imudd tawsa imi baba yella ixeddem di ṣṣeḥra deg unẓul n tmurt.
Akken i d-kecmeɣ tameddit si teksawt, yemma tessendeh-iyi ad ssirdeɣ, ad beddleɣ iceṭṭiḍen sakin ad aliɣ ad ččeɣ imensi yerna ad muddeɣ tawsa i bab n tmeɣra.
Amek ara xedmeɣ?
Ma nniɣ ala, ilaq ad iniɣ acimi.
Ma nniɣ acimi, teɣli trugza.
Ihi, si lexbeṛ-nni, ula d lqahwa ntmeddit ur tebliɛ.
Ḥellseɣ lsiɣ iceṭṭiḍen ijdiden.
Tekmes-iyi-d yemma lkaɣeḍ n yedrimen.
Dɣa ṭṭfeɣ abrid ɣer taddart s adrar.
Iṭij yeɣli, bururu yebda yessiɣrit.
Amek akken, a Ṛebbi!
Ansa ara ɛeddiɣ akken ad awḍeɣ zik!
Abrid wezzilen, d win iɛeddan rrif n tlalat n temqebrin, ayen meṛṛa ttaggaden warrac.
Acku, timqebṛen cuddent ɣer teḥkayin yessewḥacen anida ddawaṛen iɛessasen, imeyytin, leǧnun, iderwicen.

Feḍmuca ssneɣ-tt asmi ɣriɣ aseggas amenzu deg uɣerbaz n taddart n Ɛin Mezyab.
Cfiɣ kan ass mi kecmeɣ aḍriq amenzu, lliɣ reggleɣ-d si tneɣrit.
Dɣa taselmadt tuɣal tesɣamay-iyi deg ṭṭala taneggurt deg udur aneggaru.
Akken ticki ḥelseɣ-d ad d-rewleɣ, ad tesɛu lweqt ad tazzel ad iyi-teṭṭef.
Ihi yiwet n tikkelt, akken heggeɣ iman-iw ad d-rewleɣ s axxam, Feḍmuca tebda tettɛiyyiḍ: A Massa! A Massa! A-t-an yebɣa ad yerwel.
Dɣa tacixet tuzzel-d temdel tawwurt.
Mi iɛedda lqewt, uɣeɣ tanumi d tcixet akked warrac.
Dɣa dayen uɣaleɣ ḥemmleɣ aɣerbaz.
Maca akken i iɛedda useggaz amenzu, ddiɣ ɣer uɣerbaz n taddart n Uzemmur Umeryem.
Nnejmaɛen yixeddamen zdat n Tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman.
Seld n usɛeẓẓeg n tmeẓẓuɣt n yimḍebbren n Tenmehla tazzayrit n waman ɣef wayen ssuturen ixeddamen, ladɣa timerna deg ssuma, xedmen yixeddamen-is asalag, ass n acer d arim, 6, 7 seg waggur n tubeṛ 2019.
Yella-d ula d yiwen n unejmuɛ zdat n tenmehla-agi i d-yezgan deg tlemmast n temdint n Tizi Uzzu.
Tigawt -agi timezgit n sin wussan i yal ddurt, tebda yakan seg 23 deg waggur n cutember iɛeddan, anda ssuturen aɛawed n tmuɣli deg uɣruḍ n yixeddamen anda i yettwali unmalu n yixeddamen, ddrus maḍi, u yewwi-d ad tili tmerna deg-s.
Am wakken ssutren daɣen yixeddamen-a agerrez n tewtilin n lxeddma.
Dɣa deg unejmuɛ i d-yellan zdat n tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman, heḍren-d yixeddamen aṭas ɣef yiɣeblan i d-ttmagaren deg yimeḍqan n uxeddim, yettilin deg lḥers meqqren deg kra n tegnatin, zdat n lɣiḍ n yimezdaɣ.
Ɣef leḥsab n yimḍebbren n unmalu, lexṣas n ttawilat iwatan yeɛgeb aṭas axeddim, dayen i d-yettawin iɣeblan meqqren deg uxeddim.
Nnan-d yimeḍebbren n tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman d akken s kra n wayen ssutren ixeddamen, d ayen yellan d sswab, d azref, maca ur zmiren ara ad xedmen acemma, dayen yeffɣen i lebɣi-nsen, imi d aɣbel yeɛnan yakk tamurt n Zzayer.
Zdat n usɛeẓẓeg n tmeẓẓuɣt i tikkelt-nniḍen n yimḍebbren teɛna temsalt, kecmen yixeddamen n tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman deg yiwen usalag war aneḥbus alamma rran-d yimḍebbren teɛna temsalt ɣer tuget n wayen ssutren.
Yella umaru ameɣnas Allas Di Tlelli, ass n 5 tuber yezrin, ɣef 14 :00, d inebgi n temlilit taseklant i d-tettheyyi tiddukla Azday n Uwqas deg unammas adelsan Reḥmani Sliman.
S uzwel n "Taqbaylit: d acu-ten yiberdan akkin i tezɣint n Lezzayer?", yewwi-d awal ɣef tekliwin tiɣerfanin i d-yettilin yal sem i yettwali beɛdent akken ad asent-nsemmi "tagrawla".
"Ɣur-i nekk d tasmessit meqqren kan, imi ulac deg-s tigejda n umussu asertan neɣ dɣa n tegrawla, am wayen icban udem neɣ takza, taɣessa, arkawalen yettwarun, taferkit n ubrid iccuden, iswan usdiden", i d-yenna.
Yerna yenna-d ɣef waya d akken, "d aya merra i yeǧǧan 33 n tikliwin i d-yellan yal ass n sem, d tid ur d-newwi kra d tarennawt i umennuɣ ɣef tugdut n tilawt imi teqqim-d kan di ccnawi s taεrabt ula di tmurt taqbaylit".
Ɣur Mass Allas Di Tlelli, "yewwi-d ad d-yili umeslay ɣef timsal tigejdanin icudden ɣer usenfaṛ n tmetti ara yettwasbedden deg umḍiq n udabu, ma yella yeɣli, am wayen yecban taggara n usεuṛṛeb n uɣerbaz d tedbelt, talakt d tlelliyin akken ma llant", i iwala.
Gar cwiṭ d waṭas, yebder-d daɣen umsarag taluft n ubrid iwulmen n umennuɣ d wamek ilaq ad d-yelmed yal yiwen seg temsirin Ɛimac Ɛmer, Bennay Wali, Masin Uharun, Agraw n Yimaziɣen, tanekra n Tefsut n 1980.
Ugar n waya, yettwawi-d wawal ula ɣef taluft n yisluguten i yettwaddamen da d din, d yinumak yemgaraden i d-ttakken gar Tmurt n Yiqbayliyen d temnaḍin-nniḍen n Zzayer, d wamek i yessefk si tura ad imuqel yal yiwen ɣef ubrid d tifrat tisertanin ara yeffɣen fell-as.
Seld inaw-is, yella-d uskasi akked yimeḥḍar i d-yusan s ṭṭaqa ass-nni.
Yemmut yiwen n unelmad deg uɣerbaz.
Kkren-d yimezdaɣ n tɣiwant n Buεendas ass n, 6 tubeṛ yezrin, ɣef ṣṣut n leεyaḍ d yimeṭṭawen n warrac d yimawlan-nsen.
Ayagi imi i d-yeɣli yiwen n uɣrab deg uɣerbaz alemmas Ɛli Zermani.
D win i d-yezgan di tɣiwant n Buεendas, deg waɣir n Sṭif.
Γef leḥsab n yisallen i aɣ-d-yewwḍen, axeṣṣaṛ-a i yeḍṛan deg texxamin n ubduz, yegla s terwiḥt n yiwen n unelmad.
Ma yella d inelmaden-nniḍen i yellan deg wadeg-nni imir-n, jerḥen, yerna addad-nsen mačči d win yeṣṣefṛaḥen.
Ineggura-a, ttwawin s uɣiwel i teklinikt n Buεendas.
Ad d-nesmekti d akken ula d taklinikt-a, hrurin leḥyuḍ-is, dɣa ula d nettat seg teswiεt ɣer tayeḍ, zemren ad d-ɣlin, ladɣa imi lebni-is d aqbuṛ nezzeh.
Seg tama n yimezdaɣ, irkeb-iten zzεef d ameqqṛan, imi ayen yeḍṛan d lemri ɣef waddad n tɣiwant n Buεendas i yuɣalen di rrif seg yal tama.
Ula d aselḥu n tlufa deg-s, ur yewqim ara.
Ayagi imi imasayen n uɣerbaz-a alemmas, ṣṣawḍen-asen i yimḍebbṛen n tɣiwant isallen ɣef umahi ideg ttidiren warrac deg uɣerbaz-a.
Yerna mačči d aɣrab-nni i d-yeɣlin i yehṛuran kan, ula d yiwen-nniḍen seg wid i d-yezzin i tesnawit, ur yettεeṭṭil ara ad d-yernu iɣer gma-s.
Meḥsub nezmer ad d-nini, amahi yezzi-asen i yinelmaden, nutni zgan-d di tlemmast.
War ma yesseḥseb yiwen i wayen i izemren ad yeḍṛu.
Asteqsi-nneɣ ass-a, d anwa i ilaq ad sḍelmen?
D anemhal i yeǧǧan arrac tezzin ɣer umkan-nni, ur nesεi taɣellist, neɣ d ibabaten n warrac i yestehzan, ssusmen ɣef wayen iḍuṛṛen i dderya-nsen?
Neɣ d tamurt i yefkan azal i wayen ur neswi, ma d arraw-is swan seg yidammen-nsen?
Yal yiwen itekka deg txeṣṣaṛṭ-a, lameεna lemḍeṛṛa-s d ineglusen i tt-ixellṣen.
Aseqqamu aɣerfan n Tizi Uzzu yessuter akemmel n yisenfaren yettwaḥebsen.
Gar yisenfaren iɣessanen i mazal ttwaɛelqen ar ass-a deg ugezdu n Tizi Uzzu, ad naf annar n ddabax n uḍar n 50 000 n yimeḍqan, tawdeft ɣer ubrid ameqqran n usamer amalu, aggugen n Sidi Xlifa d Tizi n Tlata, Isseɣser n usizdeg n waman, sbiṭer n 500 n yimṭerḥen, axxam n tujjya n tlawin d warrac.
Yeẓdem-d wuccen ɣef taddart.
Seld taluft n yimcac isaḍen, i d-igan ma drus 6 n yimejraḥ, ddren ussan-a kan yimezdaɣ n temnaḍt n Tigratin, taddart n At Tɛisiwt, rrehba-nniḍen i icudden ɣer yiwen n wuccen i d-iẓedmen ɣef umḍiq n uzedduɣ.
D ayen ur d-neḍri seg waṭas n yiseggasen tura, imi uccen d win yettaggaden amdan, ur d-yettqerrib ɣer wanida caḍent tnezduɣin.
Maca tikkelt-a, ɣef rray amatu n medden, d laẓ i yeǧǧan uccen ad yettcali ɣer unadi n tgella armi d tasebḥit, war ma iga i yiman-is tilas.
Dɣa, mi d-iɛedda yiwen n yilemẓi si tama n tebḥirt, yesla i usuɣu i yeffɣen i leɛwayed. Armi iwala d uccen, yessawel i temɛiwna n lɣaci akken ad t-id-ṭṭfen.
Ayen yesḥissifen, d taɣara amek i as-lḥan yimezdaɣ i taluft d wamek nɣan uccen-a amraɛ.
Acku, seld mi as-reglen kra n yimdanen akk tizerbatin n trewla, kkaten-t s yiblaḍen armi yefcel, syinna kemmlen-as s yiɛekkazen armi yemmut.
Uccen-nni yella yettgabar kra meskud ur yeqqim deg umkan-is n tudert, di lexla, ulamma yuli wass.
Cwi kan nessaweḍ neddukkel, nenɣa-t war iɣilifen, acku yella d amihi ama i warrac, i yimeqqranen neɣ i yiɣersiwen-nneɣ.
Ad d-nesmekti d akken ssawlen yiɣermanen i yimḍebbren n tɣiwant n At Smaɛel uɣur sutren awelleh mi nɣan dayen aɣersiw-nni.
Dɣa, nnan-asen yimasayen ilaq kan ad meḍlen agectum n wuccen akken ur t-yettaweḍ uɣersiw nniḍen, ur d-yettili usedreɛ n kra n waṭṭanen ma yella yuḍen.
Imir-nni i ddmen yilemẓiyen lǧifa n wuccen, wwin-tt ɣer wadeg yexlan, meḍlen-tt deg teɣder n wakal.
Akken netteg deg tfelwa-nni n zik sut kraḍ n wudmawen, reqqmeɣ-d da, i unecṛah-inu yezgan deg wul, tisirit-nni i aɣ-d-yewwi Sidna Ɛisa deg yiwet n teqsiḍt.

Ass-a iṣḥa yigenni.
Teṣḥa tegnawt ass-a.
Muddeɣ-d asarag ɣef tutlayt taqbaylit.
Ddiɣ ass-a ad ɣreɣ tamsirt ɣef yilugan n tira.
Deg Tewrirt Musa, ilul uqcic d amencuf.
Limmer mazal yeddir, tili ass-a, ɣur-s 64 n yiseggasen deg leɛmer-is.
Am yal aseggas, tesmekta-d taddart-is, Tawrirt Musa Waɛmer, ass-nni n lǧemɛa, 24 deg yennayer 2020, talalit n Meɛtub Lwennas.
Heggan-d tameɣra s kra n leqdicat idelsanen..
Am wakken i d-rzan aṭas n yimdanen, am tannumi, ɣer uẓekka-s seg yal tama n Tmurt.
Aṭas n tejmilin, diɣ, i as-yuɣal ama deg Tmurt neɣ deg beṛṛa.
Llant-d temsikniyin, isaragen d wayen-nniḍen.
Semman ula d kra n yimekwan s yisem-is.
Ilul Matub Lwennas ass n, 24 deg yennayer 1956, deg taddart n Tewrirt Musa Waɛmer n lɛarc n At Dwala.
Seg wasmi i d-yekker, netta d amennuɣ: ur yelli kra i as-d-yusan kan akka. Yal tallit deg tudert-is, yefka-as lkar-is.
Seg wasmi yella d agrud armi yettwanɣa ass n, 25 deg yulyu 1998, deg Tala Bbunan, netta d amqelleɛ.
Anta ur yesɛedda mi yella d agrud, temẓi akked tgiṭar, Tafsut n yimaziɣen, tuber 1988, tukerḍa-s sɣur ugraw ineslem yettwaselḥen armi d timenɣiwt-is deg useggas n 1998.
Yecna Lwennas Meɛtub i tikkelt taneggarut deg tzeqqa tameqqrant n Zenith n Fransa ass n, 12 deg yennayer 1998.
Yettunefk-as warraz n tmektit sɣur Danielle Mitterrand deg useggas n 1994.
Seg tama n tiktiwin, nezmer ad d-nini, yettagem-d Meɛtub s umata deg tliwa-agi: Tamurt, taddart akked yiman-is.
Seg tama n uẓawan n ccaɛbi, yesseqdac akk ṭṭbuɛ am Zzidan, Ssika, Ṛresd, Ṛmel maya…atg.
Rnu ɣer waya, yura adlis le Rebelle i d-yessufeɣ deg useggas n 1996, sin n yiseggas kan uqbel ad yemmet, sin-nniḍen daɣen mbeɛd mi yettwaker deg useggas 1994.
Aṭas i yuran daɣen fell-as.
Am wakken i d-llan yinadiyen, tizrawin akked usuqel ɣef ccna-s.

Uqbel ad iyi-d-tefkem ṛṛay-nwen, Ha-tt-ah tmuɣli-w.
D acu kan, uqbel ad d-aruɣ ṛṛay-iw, bɣiɣ ad d-iniɣ belli llan 03 n yiberdan akken ad iwali yiwen ma lhant neɣ ur lhint ara tezlatin n uḍebsi-agi aneggaru.
Abrid amezwaru ad iwali yiwen tizlatin n uḍebsi-agi deg yiman-nsent.
Ad iẓer ma ččurent-as allen neɣ xuṣṣent.
Lmeɛna-s, mebla ma ikenna-tent, la ɣer tezlatin-nniḍen n Zeddek la ɣer tid n yicennayen wiyaḍ.
Ad tent-yewzen ilmend kan n wayen i refdent d ccbaḥa d unamek.
Ittusemma ad yektil azal-nsent deg wayen i as-d-ibanen izad neɣ yenqes.
Yal yiwet deg-sent iman-is, deg wazal-is deg yiman-is.
Deg ubrid-agi amezwaru, ad d-yini unermas ṛṛay-is ɣef yiḍrisen d uẓawan n tezlatin, ad d-yini ma ɛeǧbent-as tezlatin neɣ ala.
Abrid wis sin, ad iwali yiwen tizlatin-agi ma ddant d uɣanib s wayes yettwassen lmulud Zeddek, abeɛda deg yiseggasen-agi ineggura.
Ittusemma d akenni ara tent-ikenni unermas, d amseflid neɣ d ameɣri, ɣer tezlatin tiqdimin.
Deg ukenni-agi ara tili tririt ɣef usteqsi ma lhant tezlatin n uḍebsi-agi neɣ xaṭi
Di tmuɣli-agi, ad ttwaktalent tizlatin s lmizan n wayen yessen yakan unermas di ccna n Lmulud Zeddek .
Deg-s ad yeɛreḍ ad inadi ma rnant-d kra ɣer wayen yellan yakan ɣer ucennay-agi.
Dagi ara nẓer ma qqimen yiberdan n usnulfu d widen yellan yakan ɣer umesnulfuy-agi neɣ beddlen.
Deg ubrid-agi wis sin, yezmer ad d-yini unermas ṛṛay-is ɣef tezlatin n uḍebsi-agi amaynut akka.
Tizlatin-agi, lhant acku ddant d uɣanib n Lmulud Zeddek, nennum-itent akkenni.

Nekk d ajenyuṛ seg Uɣerbaz Aɣelnaw Unnig n Tsenselkimt n Zzayer.
Fukkeɣ deg waggur-agi n yunyu asenfaṛ-iw n taggara n tezrawt s uzwel: "Aɛqal n taɣect yettwabnan ɣef ulmad alqayan i tutlayt taqbaylit".
D yiwet n tetiknikt tamaynut i neseqdac ass-a deg uḥric n tigzi n tmacint.
Ddeqs aya segmi ttekkaɣ deg yisenfaṛen akk n usideg akked usimḍen.
Ama d isenfaṛen n tesbeddit Mozilla am Common Voice, ama d Tatoeba neɣ d asideg n tɣerɣarin tumḍinin.
Imi lliɣ d anelmad n tsenselkimt, tteɛṛaḍeɣ ad d-awiɣ ayen i wumi zemreɣ, yal mi ara stafiɣ.
Seg wannect-n, gziɣ acu i d azal i zemren wallalen akk n tsenselkimt ad t-id-awin i usebded d usnerni n tutlayt, abeɛda tutlayt-nneɣ taqbaylit.
Tɛedda tallit i deg d tira i d allal amezwaru i s ara tesnerniḍ tutlayt.
Ass-a, imdanen ur qqaṛen ara annect i iwehha wallaɣ-nsen ɣer tilifun neɣ Internet.
Ɣef waya, anekcum n teqbaylit ɣer umaḍal umḍin, yufrar-d gar ttawilat akk i yes-s nezmer ad nesbedd tutlayt-nneɣ.
Asmi i d-iwweḍ lawan ad ferneɣ asenfaṛ n taggara n tezrawt, nwiɣ ad xedmeɣ deg wayen akk icudden ɣer yisenfaṛen-agi n usideg i yebdan yakan.
Uriɣ-as i Mass Muḥend Belqasem, d ajenyuṛ iqeddcen ayen dinn deg unnar n usideg.
Nemlal, nemmeslay acḥal d abrid. Nmuqel anwa asenfar i izemren ad ittwaxdem akka tura, dɣa nefren-d wagi : "Aɛqal n taɣect yettwabnan ɣef ulmad alqayan i tutlayt teqbaylit ".

Kra nniḍen qqaṛen-d: Yenni, d isem n umdan amezwaru i d-yusan ar temnaḍt-a.

Syen akkin, mi d-yerra akk tamurt-is, ittekka s yiserdasen-ines deg umennuɣ ameqqran n Zama mgal Anibal.
Taqbaylit ass-a,tger aṭas n yisurifen ɣer zdat.
Nedder almi i tettwaru s wallalen atraren.
Aya yell-ad s leqdic d leɛtab n wid iwumi tella deg wul.
